function getCookie(name){

var dc = document.cookie; 
var prefix = name + "=";
var begin = dc.indexOf("; " + prefix);

if (begin == -1) 
{        
    begin = dc.indexOf(prefix); 
    if (begin != 0) return null;
}else{ 
    begin += 2; 
}

var end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", begin);

if (end == -1){ 
    end = dc.length;
} 
  return unescape(dc.substring(begin + prefix.length, end));
}

jQuery('#make').val("");

}		
$(window).bind("load", function() {
$('#research a').click(function(){
		switch_tabs($(this));
		$(this).next().find('span.act').css('display:','block');
	});
	resetSearchWidget();
	switch_tabs($('.defaulttab')); 
});	
function switch_tabs(obj)
{
	$('.reasearchboxinner').hide();
	$('#research a').removeClass("current");
	var id = obj.attr("rel");
	$('#'+id).delay(200).fadeTo("slow", 1);
	obj.addClass("current");
}

function hideLoaderEtc() {
	$('#deals').hide();
	$("#deals_in_spacer").hide();
	$("#deals_in").hide();
	$("#deals_in_close").hide();
	$('#loading, #hideByACar').hide();
	$("#searchdiscounts").val("Type a car name");

}


function getModelVariant(val, flag, isNew,vtype){	
	var tisNew=isNew;
	if(tisNew==2)tisNew="";
	jQuery.post('http://www.zigwheels.com/2db/getmodelvariant.php', {'val':val, 'flag': flag, 'isNew': tisNew,'vtype':vtype}, function(data){
		if(flag=='model' && isNew==1){
			jQuery('#model').html(data);
		}else if(flag=='model' && isNew==2){
			jQuery('#byBrandModel').html(data);
		}else{
			jQuery('#bikemodel').html(data);
		}
	});
}

function getDealerCity(cityname){	
	if(cityname != ''){
		
		$('#loading_d_c').show();
		jQuery.post('http://www.zigwheels.com/2db/dealerMake2db.php', {'getcity':1, 'city':cityname}, function(data){
			jQuery('#dealercity').html(data);
			$('#dealercity').val(cityname);
				
			jQuery.post('http://www.zigwheels.com/2db/dealerMake2db.php', {'city':cityname, 'getmake':1}, function(data){
				jQuery('#dealermake').html(data);
				$('#loading_d_c').hide();
				$('#dealer').show();			
			});		
			
		});
	}
}

function getDealerMake(cityname){	
	if(cityname != ''){
		$('#dealercity0').val(cityname);
		$('#loading_d_m').show();
		jQuery.post('http://www.zigwheels.com/2db/dealerMake2db.php', {'city':cityname, 'getmake':1}, function(data){
				jQuery('#dealermake').html(data);
				$('#loading_d_m').hide();
						
			});		
			
		
	} else {
		jQuery('#dealermake').html('<option value="">Select Make</option>');
	}
}


function getSellCarData(val){
		var flag=0;
		var year=$('#newyear').val();
		var month=$('#newmonth').val();
		var city=$('#newcity').val();
		var make=$('#newmake').val();
		var model=$('#newmodel').val();
		var variant=$('#newvariant').val();
		
		

		if(year!="" && month!="" && city!=""){
			if(make==""){
				flag=1;
			}else if(val=='make'){
				flag=2;
				$('#newvariant').html('<option value="">Select Variant</option>');
			}else if(val=='model'){
				flag=3;

			}
			if(flag!=0){
				$.post(CMSROOTPATH+'/getsellcardata.php',{'year':year, 'month':month,'make':make, 'model':model, 'variant':variant, 'flag':flag, 'city': city}, function(data){
					 if(flag==1){
							$('#newmake').html(data);
							 
					 }else if(flag==2){
							$('#newmodel').html(data);
							
					 }else if(flag==3){
							$('#newvariant').html(data);
							
					 }
				});
			}
		}
}

function checkSellCarValidation(){
	var city=jQuery('#newcity').val();
	var make=jQuery('#newmake').val();
	var model=jQuery('#newmodel').val();
	
	
	var variant=jQuery('#newvariant').val();
	var year=jQuery('#newyear').val();
	var month=jQuery('#newmonth').val();
	var message;
	
	var flag=0;
	jQuery('#sellcarerrorpalceholder').hide();
	if(city==""){
		message="Please select your City";
		jQuery('#sellcarerrorpalceholder').css('display','block');
		jQuery('#sellcarerrorpalceholder').html(message);
		jQuery('#newcity').focus();
		flag=1;		
	}else if(make==""){
		message="Please select your Make";
		jQuery('#sellcarerrorpalceholder').css('display','block');
		jQuery('#sellcarerrorpalceholder').html(message);
		jQuery('#newmake').focus();
		flag=1;		
	}else if(model==""){
		message="Please select your Model";
		jQuery('#sellcarerrorpalceholder').css('display','block');
		jQuery('#sellcarerrorpalceholder').html(message);
		jQuery('#newmodel').focus();
		flag=1;		
	}else if(variant==""){
		message="Please select your Variant";
		jQuery('#sellcarerrorpalceholder').css('display','block');
		jQuery('#sellcarerrorpalceholder').html(message);
		jQuery('#newvariant').focus();
		flag=1;			
	}else if(year==""){
		message="Please select Year for which you want market price";
		jQuery('#sellcarerrorpalceholder').css('display','block');
		jQuery('#sellcarerrorpalceholder').html(message);
		jQuery('#newyear').focus();
		flag=1;		
	}else if(month==""){
		message="Please select Month for which you want market price";
		jQuery('#sellcarerrorpalceholder').css('display','block');
		jQuery('#sellcarerrorpalceholder').html(message);
		jQuery('#newmonth').focus();
		flag=1;		
	}		
	
	if(flag==0){
		jQuery.post('http://www.zigwheels.com/2db/putlead.php',{"CITYID":city, "MANUFACTURER_ID":make, "MODEL_ID":model, "VARIANT_ID":variant, "MAKEYEAR":year, "MAKEMONTH": month,"LEAD_TYPE_ID":2,"VEHICALTYPE":'4Wheeler'},function(data){
		/*$('#showmarketvalue1').html(data);
		$("#showmarketvalue1").show();
	     $("#showmarketvalue").hide();*/
		 jQuery("#showmarketvalue").hide();
		 jQuery("#showmarketvalue1").show();
		 jQuery('#showmarketvalue1').html(data);
		});
	}	
}

function checkSellCarUpdateValidation(){
	var sellcarname=jQuery('#sellcarname').val();
	var sellcarmobile=jQuery('#sellcarmobile').val();
	var sellCarID=jQuery('#sellcarleadid').val();
	var crmsellCarID=jQuery('#crmsellcarleadid').val();
        var receive_call=jQuery('#receive_call').val();
	if(document.getElementById('receive_call').checked==false)
	{  receive_call=0;
	}else
	{
	 receive_call=1;
	}
	jQuery('#sellcarerrorpalceholder').hide();
	var flag=0;
	var message;
	if(sellcarname==""){
		message="Please Enter your Name";
		jQuery('#sellcarerrorpalceholder').css('display','block');
		jQuery('#sellcarerrorpalceholder').html(message);
		jQuery('#sellcarname').focus();
		flag=1;		
  	}else if(isNaN(sellcarmobile) || sellcarmobile.length < 10){
		message="Please Enter a valid Mobile Number.";
		jQuery('#sellcarerrorpalceholder').css('display','block');
		jQuery('#sellcarerrorpalceholder').html(message);
		jQuery('#sellcarmobile').focus();
		flag=1;		
	}else if(!isalphabetic(sellcarname)){
		message="Please enter a valid Name.";
		jQuery('#sellcarerrorpalceholder').css('display','block');
		jQuery('#sellcarerrorpalceholder').html(message);
		jQuery('#sellcarname').focus();
		flag=1;	
	}
//	alert(flag);
	if(flag==0){
		jQuery.post('http://www.zigwheels.com/2db/putlead.php',{"name":sellcarname, "mobile":sellcarmobile,"crmsellCarID":crmsellCarID ,"sellCarID":sellCarID ,flag:'update',"ZIG_CALL":receive_call,"VEHICALTYPE":'4Wheeler'},function(data){ //alert(data);
			$('#showmarketvalue1').html(data);
			$("#showmarketvalue1").show();
			$("#showmarketvalue").hide();
		});
	}

}

function redirectToDealer(){
	
	var city=jQuery('#dealercity').val();
	
	var w =document.getElementById('dealermake').selectedIndex;		//alert(w);
	var make =document.getElementById('dealermake').options[w].text;
	
	if(make=='Select Make')	{
		alert('Please Select Make');
		jQuery('#dealermake').focus();
		return false;
	}
	else if (city==''){
		alert('Please Select your city First');
		jQuery('#dealercity').focus();
		return false;
	}
	else{
		var makeName = make.replace(/-/g, "~");
		makeName = makeName.replace(/ /g, "-");
		var cityName = city.replace(/ /g, "-");
		//window.location.href='http://www.zigwheels.com/dealers.php?incity='+city+'&make='+makeName;
		window.location.href= 'http://www.zigwheels.com/dealers/'+makeName+'/'+cityName;
	}
}



function redirectToMakeModelPage(){

	var w =document.getElementById('make').selectedIndex;		//alert(w);
	var make =document.getElementById('make').options[w].text;
	
	var w1 =document.getElementById('model').selectedIndex;		//alert(w);
	var model =document.getElementById('model').options[w1].text;

	var makeName = make.replace("-", "~");
		makeName = makeName.replace(/ /g, "-");
	//alert(makeName+model);
	if(model!="Model"){	
		var modelName = model.replace("-", "~") ;
		modelName = modelName.replace(/ /g, "-");
		var url='http://www.zigwheels.com/newcars/'+makeName+'/'+modelName;
	}else{
		var url='http://www.zigwheels.com/newcars/'+makeName;
	}
	if(make!="Make"){
		window.location.href=url;
	}
	else{
	
		jQuery('#selectmakeerrorpalceholder').html("No manufacturer selected.");
		jQuery('#selectmakeerrorpalceholder').show();
		jQuery('#orImageSeperator').hide();
		setTimeout(function(){jQuery('#selectmakeerrorpalceholder').hide();jQuery('#orImageSeperator').show();},5000);
	}
}

function redirectToSearchResults(){
	var from_price=jQuery('#from_price').val();
	var to_price=jQuery('#to_price').val();
	
	if(parseFloat(to_price) <= parseFloat(from_price)){
		alert('Select valid price range.');
		return;
	}	
	var byshowroomprice=from_price+'-'+to_price; //alert(byshowroomprice);
	window.location.href='http://www.zigwheels.com/newcarsearchresult.php?pg=1&byshowroomprice='+byshowroomprice;
}

function showSearchResuls(val, e){
	
	var charCode;    
    if(e && e.which){
        charCode = e.which;
    }else if(window.event){
        e = window.event;
        charCode = e.keyCode;
    }
	if(val.length >= 2){
		$('#blockByACar').removeClass('brd');
		$('#blockByACar').addClass('brdblak');
		$('#loading, #hideByACar').show();
		$("#deals_in_close").show();

		var pos = $("#deals_parent").position();
		var top = pos.top;
		var left = pos.left;
		$("#deals").css({position:'absolute', top:top+'px', left:left+'px'});
		
		jQuery.post('/2db/gethomepagetabsearchresults.php', {'val':val,'source':'home'}, function(data){
			//alert(data);
			//set postion;

			$('#loading, #hideByACar').hide();
			$('#deals, #deals_in_spacer').show();
			$('#deals_in, #deals_in_close').show();
			$('#deals_in').html(data);
			
		});
	}
}
$(function(){
	$('#make').focus();
});
function searchByBrand(){
	var cityId=jQuery.trim(jQuery('#byPriceCity').val());
	var makeId=jQuery.trim(jQuery('#byBrandMake').val());
	var ModelId=jQuery.trim(jQuery('#byBrandModel').val());


	var url='';
	if(cityId=='' && makeId==''){
		message="Please Select atleast one field for search.";
		alert(message)
		jQuery('#byPriceCity').focus();
		return false;
	}
	if(cityId!=""){
		url+="&bycity="+cityId;			
	}
	if(makeId!=""){
			url+="&bymakeid="+makeId;			
	}
	if(ModelId!="" && ModelId!=null){
		url+="&bymodelid="+ModelId;			
	}
	window.location.href='usedcarsearchresult.php?pg=1'+url;
	return true;
}
function searchById(){
    var listingId=jQuery('#byBrandListingId').val();
	var url='';
	var flag=0;
	if(listingId=='' || listingId=='Search by Listing ID' ){
		message="Please Enter  listing ID .";
		alert(message)
		flag=1;
		return false;
	}
	if(flag==0){
		jQuery.post('http://www.zigwheels.com/checkUsedlisting.php',{"listingid":listingId},function(data){ 
			if(data.toString()=="0"){
				alert("Sorry No data found for this listing id");
			}
			else{
				url+="listingid="+listingId;	
				window.location.href='usedcarlistingdetails.php?'+url;
			}	
		});
	}
	return true;
}
function searchByPrice(){
	var cityId=jQuery.trim(jQuery('#byPriceCity').val());
	var fromprice=jQuery.trim(jQuery('#usedcarfrom_price').val());
	var toprice=jQuery.trim(jQuery('#usedcarto_price').val());
	var priceRange='';
	var url='';
	if(cityId=='' && (fromprice==0 || toprice==0)){
		message="Please select at least city or price range for search.";
		alert(message)
		jQuery('#usedcarfrom_price').focus();
		return false;
	}
	if(parseFloat(toprice) <= parseFloat(fromprice)){
		alert('Select valid price range.');
		return;
	}	
	if(cityId!=""){
		url+="&bycity="+cityId;			
	}
	if(fromprice!=0 && toprice!=0){
		url+="&budget="+fromprice+"-"+toprice;			
	}	
	window.location.href='usedcarsearchresult.php?pg=1'+url;
	return true;
}

function resultByBrand(){
	var make=jQuery("#bikemake").val();
	var model=jQuery("#bikemodel").val();
	var w =document.getElementById('bikemake').selectedIndex;		//alert(w);
	var makeName =document.getElementById('bikemake').options[w].text;
	var w1 =document.getElementById('bikemodel').selectedIndex;		//alert(w);
	var modelName =document.getElementById('bikemodel').options[w1].text;
	if(make==''){
		alert("Please select Brand");
		jQuery('#bikemake').focus();
	}else if(model!=''){ 
		var makeName1=makeName.replace(/\ /g, '-');
		var modelName1=modelName.replace(/\ /g, '-');
		window.location.href= 'http://www.zigwheels.com/newbikes/'+makeName1+"/"+modelName1;
	}else{
		window.location.href= 'http://www.zigwheels.com/newbikesearchresult.php?vichle_type=2Wheeler&limit=10&pg=1&sortdirection=asc&bymakeid='+make;
	}
}


function resultByPrice(){
	var fromPrice=jQuery("#bikefrom_price").val();
	var toPrice=jQuery("#biketo_price").val();
	if(fromPrice==''){ alert("Please Select Min Price"); jQuery('#bikefrom_price').focus();}
	else if(toPrice==''){ alert("Please Select Max Price"); jQuery('#biketo_price').focus();}
	else if(parseInt(fromPrice) > parseInt(toPrice)){ alert("Please select valid price range"); jQuery('#biketo_price').focus();}
	else if(parseInt(fromPrice) == parseInt(toPrice)){ alert("Please select valid price range");jQuery('#biketo_price').focus();}
	else{
		window.location.href= 'http://www.zigwheels.com/newbikesearchresult.php?vichle_type=2Wheeler&byshowroomprice='+fromPrice+'-'+toPrice+'&bycity=Delhi&limit=10&pg=1&sortdirection=asc';
	}
	
}
function resultByEngineCC(){
var engineCC=jQuery("#byenginecapacity").val();
if(engineCC==''){
	alert("Please select Engine CC");
	jQuery('#byenginecapacity').focus();
	}else{
		window.location.href= 'http://www.zigwheels.com/newbikesearchresult.php?vichle_type=2Wheeler&byenginepower='+engineCC;
	}
}

<script language="javascript">
function str_replace (search, replace, subject, count) {
    var i = 0,
        j = 0,
        temp = '',
        repl = '',
        sl = 0,
        fl = 0,
        f = [].concat(search),
        r = [].concat(replace),
        s = subject,
        ra = Object.prototype.toString.call(r) === '[object Array]',
        sa = Object.prototype.toString.call(s) === '[object Array]';
    s = [].concat(s);
    if (count) {
        this.window[count] = 0;
    }

    for (i = 0, sl = s.length; i < sl; i++) {
        if (s[i] === '') {
            continue;
        }
        for (j = 0, fl = f.length; j < fl; j++) {
            temp = s[i] + '';
            repl = ra ? (r[j] !== undefined ? r[j] : '') : r[0];
            s[i] = (temp).split(f[j]).join(repl);
            if (count && s[i] !== temp) {
                this.window[count] += (temp.length - s[i].length) / f[j].length;
            }
        }
    }
    return sa ? s : s[0];
}

function getByHeaderSearch(){
	//changes made by marghoob suleman
	var bysearch=jQuery('#byHomeHeaderSearch').val();
	bysearch = encodeURI(bysearch.replace(/\s/ig, "+"));
	window.location.href= "http://www.zigwheels.com/contentsearch.php?bysearch="+bysearch;	
}
function searchHandleEnter(inField, e){
    var charCode;    
    if(e && e.which){
        charCode = e.which;
    }else if(window.event){
        e = window.event;
        charCode = e.keyCode;
    }
  if(charCode == 13) {
        getByHeaderSearch();
    }
}
$(document).ready(function(){
	$('#byHomeHeaderSearch').bind('keypress', function(e) {
	var code = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
	 if(code == 13) { //Enter keycode
	   //Do something
	   getByHeaderSearch();
	 }
	});
});
</script>

function printTicketId(data){

function checkZWLoginStatus(){
	var userType =  Get_Cookie('user_type');
	if(userType==null){
		return 0;
	}
	else{
		return 1;
	}
}
function reloadWindow(){
	if($.browser.safari){
		// there is no any specific way to detect chrome browser.
		var url = Get_Cookie("bookmark");
		del_cookie("bookmark", '/', '');
		parent.window.opener.location.href = url;
		
	}else if($.browser.msie){
		// no need to do any thing already event is attached in popup function.
	}else{
		try{
			//window.parent.location.href=document.referrer;
			var url = Get_Cookie("bookmark");
			del_cookie("bookmark", '/', '');
			parent.window.opener.location.href = url;
		}catch(e){
			//alert(e.message);
			parent.window.opener.location.href = 'http://www.zigwheels.com';	
		}
	}

}
function setRedirectionCookiesforIe(url){ 
	if($.browser.msie){ 
		Set_Cookie("bookmark",url,'','/','','');
	}
}
function gplushRedirectUrl(url){
	if($.browser.safari){
		// there is no any specific way to detect chrome browser.
		//var url = Get_Cookie("bookmark");
		del_cookie("bookmark", '/', '');
		parent.window.opener.location.href = url;
		
	}else if($.browser.msie){
		// no need to do any thing already event is attached in popup function.
	}else{
		try{
			//window.parent.location.href=document.referrer;
			//var url = Get_Cookie("bookmark");
			del_cookie("bookmark", '/', '');
			parent.window.opener.location.href = url;
		}catch(e){
			//alert(e.message);
			parent.window.opener.location.href = 'http://www.zigwheels.com';	
		}
	}self.close(); 
}
function redirectUrl(url){
	if($.browser.msie){
		Set_Cookie("bookmark",url,'','/','','');
		self.close();
	}else{
		if(checkZWLoginStatus()==1){window.parent.location.href=url;}
		self.close();
	}
}
function redirectToDealerRegistration(){
	var url ='http://www.zigwheels.com/dealer-packages';
	if($.browser.msie){
		Set_Cookie("bookmark",url,'','/','','');
		self.close();
	}else{
		parent.window.opener.location.href = url;
		//window.parent.location.href=url;
		self.close();
	}
}
function loginCookies(dataarray){
	Set_Cookie("USERID",dataarray[1],'','/','','');
	Set_Cookie("USER_ID",dataarray[1],'','/','','');
	Set_Cookie("NAME",dataarray[2],'','/','','');
	Set_Cookie("LOGINNAME",dataarray[2],'','/','','');
	Set_Cookie("EMAIL",dataarray[3],'','/','','');
	Set_Cookie("USERTYPE",dataarray[4],'','/','','');
	Set_Cookie("MOBILE",dataarray[5],'','/','','');	
}
function setCookies(ticketId,autologin){
	jQuery.get('http://www.zigwheels.com/loginsuccess.php',{"ticketId":ticketId,"autologin":autologin},function(data){
		if(autologin==1)showWelcome();
	})
}
function setFacebookCookies(fb_user_id,fb_name,fb_profile_image,access_token){
	
	//var cookieDomain = ".zigwheels.com";
	Set_Cookie('fb_user_id',fb_user_id,'','/','','');
	Set_Cookie('name',fb_name,'','/','','');	
	Set_Cookie('fb_profile_image',fb_profile_image,'','/','','');
	Set_Cookie('access_token',access_token,'','/','','');
}

function deleteFacebookCookies(){
	del_cookie("fb_user_id", '/', '');
	del_cookie("name", '/', '');
	del_cookie("fb_profile_image", '/', '');
	del_cookie("access_token", '/', '');
}

function setTwitterCookies(tw_user_id,tw_name,fb_profile_image){
	Set_Cookie('tw_user_id',fb_user_id,'','/','','');
	Set_Cookie('name',tw_name,'','/','','');	
	Set_Cookie('fb_profile_image',fb_profile_image,'','/','','');
}	

function deleteTwitterCookies(){
	del_cookie("tw_user_id", '/', '');
	del_cookie("name", '/', '');
	del_cookie("fb_profile_image", '/', '');
}




function ifTwitterConnected(){
	$.getScript('http://platform.twitter.com/anywhere.js?id=bK1XAz8rgXSelE7g6FqhLA&v=1', function() {
		twttr.anywhere(function (T) {
				var currentUser = T.currentUser;
				var tw_name = currentUser.data('name');
				var tw_user_id = currentUser.data('id');
				var tw_profile_image = currentUser.data('profile_image_url');
				setTwitterCookies(tw_user_id,tw_name,tw_profile_image);
				ifTwitterUserExit(tw_user_id);
		});	
	});	
}




jQuery(function () { 
	twttr.anywhere(function (T) {
		T.bind("authComplete", function (e, user) {
			var currentUser = T.currentUser;
			var tw_name = currentUser.data('name');
			var tw_user_id = currentUser.data('id');
			var tw_profile_image = currentUser.data('profile_image_url');
			setTwitterCookies(tw_user_id,tw_name,tw_profile_image);
			var showScreen = ifTwitterUserExit(tw_user_id);	
			// triggered when auth completed successfully
		});
		if (T.isConnected()) {
			jQuery('#twlogoutdiv').show();
			//T("#login-logout").connectButton();
		 }
		else {
			T("#login-logout").connectButton();
		}
	});	
 });



function ifTwitterUserExit(tw_user_id){  
	jQuery.post('http://www.zigwheels.com/2db/validateuserReview.php',{"twuserid":tw_user_id,"submittype":"IsUserExist"},function(data){  
		dataarray=data.split('_@@@_');
		if(dataarray[0]==1){
		   //ALREADY LINKED TWITTER ACCOUNT WITH ZIGWHEELS DO LOGIN
			doAutoLogin()
			//getTwitterLoginScreen(tw_user_id,dataarray[5],'1');			
		}else if(dataarray[0]==0){
		  /// REGISTER USER SCREEN
			getTwitterLoginScreen(tw_user_id,dataarray[5]);
		}else if(dataarray[0]==3){
				jQuery('#msgholder').removeClass("error");
				jQuery('#msgholder').html("You are already registered with zigwheels.").show();	
				setTimeout(function() {jQuery('#msgholder').hide();jQuery('#msgholder').removeClass("info");jQuery('#msgholder').addClass("error");}, 5000);				
				return false;
		}else{
			getTwitterLoginScreen(tw_user_id,'');
		}
	});
} 

function doAutoLogin(reviewid){
	var fromIFrame=1;
	if(reviewid==0 || jQuery.trim(reviewid)=='undefined'){ 
		var url = Get_Cookie("bookmark"); 
		var USERTYPE = Get_Cookie("USERTYPE"); 
		//del_cookie("bookmark", '/', '');
		if(url!=null && url!="undefined" && url!=""){ 
			reloadWindow();
		}else if(USERTYPE=='Dealer'){ 
			del_cookie("bookmark", '/', '');
			Set_Cookie("bookmark","http://www.zigwheels.com/dealer-account",'','/','','');
			reloadWindow();
		}else{ 
			reloadWindow();
		}setTimeout("self.close()",1000); 
	}else{
		del_cookie("bookmark", '/', '');
		Set_Cookie("bookmark","http://www.zigwheels.com/thanks.php?clgn=1",'','/','','');
		reloadWindow();	
		setTimeout("self.close()",1000); 
	}
}
function getTwitterLoginScreen(twuserid,uemail){ 
	jQuery.get("http://www.zigwheels.com/twitterlogin.php",{"twuserid":twuserid,"email":uemail,"autologin":0}, 
		function(data){  
			jQuery('#body').html(data);
		});
}

function validateSSOForm(){ 
	jQuery('#msgholder').hide();
	jQuery('#msgholder1').hide();
	jQuery('#siteId').val('e764663e6741bcc05113a13eb7418b66');
	jQuery('#ru').val('http://www.zigwheels.com/loginsuccess.php');
	jQuery('#nru').val('http://www.zigwheels.com/userreviewlogin.php');
	var loginid=jQuery('#login').val();
	var upassword=jQuery('#passwd').val(); 
	var message;
	var flag=0;
	if( loginid == "") {
		message="Please enter email ";
		jQuery('#msgholder').html(message).show();
		jQuery('#login').focus();
		flag=1;
		return false;
	}
	else if(!isValidEmail(loginid))	{
		message="Please enter a valid Email Address.";
		jQuery('#msgholder').html(message).show();
		jQuery('#login').focus();
		flag=1;
		return false;
	}
	else if( upassword == "") {
		message="Please enter your password .";
		jQuery('#msgholder').html(message).show();
		jQuery('#passwd').focus();
		flag=1;
		return false;
	}
	jQuery('#msgholder').hide();
	
	return true;
}

function doSSOSocialMediaLogin(fb_user_id,emailID,securityKey,fb_profile_image,fb_name){
	jQuery('.email').val(emailID);
	jQuery('.firstname').val(fb_name);
	jQuery('.oauthid').val(fb_user_id);
	jQuery('.oauthsiteid').val('facebook');
	jQuery('.securitykey').val(securityKey);
	jQuery('.siteid').val('e764663e6741bcc05113a13eb7418b66');
	jQuery('.ru').val('http://www.zigwheels.com/loginsuccess.php');
	jQuery('.nru').val('http://www.zigwheels.com/userreviewlogin.php');
	jQuery('#socialmedia_login').submit();
}
// calling from toi comment form
function update_user_box(fromIFrame){

if(typeof(fromIFrame)==='undefined') fromIFrame = 0;
	//-----------------To get full permission
	FB._initialized = false;
	FB.init({
		appId      : 140130286031515,
		status     : true, 
		cookie     : true,
		xfbml      : true,
		oauth      : true
	});	
	FB.login(function(response) {
		if (response.authResponse) { 
			 updateUserBoxTOI(fromIFrame);
		} 
		else {
		  //alert('user is not logged in');
		  // user is not logged in					
		}
	}, {scope: 'email, publish_actions'} );  
	return false;	
}
function googlelogin(){
	jQuery.get("http://www.zigwheels.com/googleApi/index.php",{'googleplusurl':'google'},
	function(data){  
	var x = screen.width/2 - 900/2;
	var y = screen.height/2 - 650/2;
	popupWindowNew = window.open(data,'popupWindowNew','width=640,height=480,left='+x+',top='+y);
	});				
	return false;
}

function updateUserBoxTOI(fromIFrame){  
	var email = Get_Cookie("email");
	var fb_user_id = Get_Cookie("fb_user_id");
	//if(fb_user_id=='NaN' || fb_user_id==null || fb_user_id==0 || typeof(fb_user_id)=='undefined'){ 
		jQuery.post("http://www.zigwheels.com/tpl/tplGetFacbookUserData.php",{}, 
		function(data){  
			var x = eval("("+data+")");				
			if(x.fb_name != ""){	
				doSSOSocialMediaLogin(x.fb_user_id,x.fb_email,x.access_token,x.fb_profile_image,x.fb_name);	
				//signInOrSignUpByFacebookId(x.fb_user_id,x.fb_name,x.fb_profile_image,x.access_token,x.fb_email,fromIFrame);
				jQuery('.fbloginemaildiv').hide();
				jQuery('.socialbutton').hide();
				jQuery('.socialbutton1').show();
				
			}	
		});
	//}
}

function signInOrSignUpByFacebookId(fb_user_id,fb_name,fb_profile_image,access_token,fb_email,fromIFrame){
	if (jQuery("#fb_template").length > 0){
		jQuery('#fb_template').html("<div align=\"center\"><img src=\"http://static.zigwheels.com/images/fb-loader.gif\"/></div>");
	}	
	password=fb_email;
	usertype="Individual";
	term="Yes";
	newsletters="Yes";
	var revid=jQuery('#reviewid').val(); //alert(revid);
	jQuery('#ajaxloder').show();
	jQuery.post('http://www.zigwheels.com/2db/validateuserReview.php', {"fb_profile_image":fb_profile_image,"fb_name":fb_name,"fb_email":fb_email, "usertype":usertype,"password":password,"term":term,"newsletters":newsletters,"submittype":"facebook","reviewid":revid,"fb_user_id":fb_user_id},function(data){ 
	dataarray=data.split('_@@@_'); //alert(data);
		if(dataarray[0] == 1){
			jQuery('#msgholder').html("User already exist with same email.");	
			jQuery('#msgholder').css('display','block');
			jQuery('#temp').val('0');
		}
		else{
			//loginCookies(dataarray);
			setFacebookCookies(fb_user_id,fb_name,fb_profile_image,access_token);
			if(url!=null && url!="undefined" && url!=""){
				window.parent.location.href = url;
			}
			else if(dataarray[4]=='Dealer'){
				window.parent.location.href = "dealer-account";
			}
			else{
				if(fromIFrame==1){
					window.parent.location.href=document.referrer;
				}
				else{
					window.location.reload();
				}
			}
		}
	});
}

function zwsignOut(){
	jQuery.post('http://www.zigwheels.com/logout.php',{"zwlogout":"1"},function(data){
			showWelcome();
	});
	del_cookie('fb_user_id', '/', '');
	del_cookie('access_token', '/', '');
	del_cookie('user_type', '/', '');
	
}

function signOut(){
	if(Get_Cookie("fb_user_id") != ''){
		deleteFacebookCookies();
		FB.getLoginStatus(function(response) {
			if (response.status === 'connected'){
				FB.logout(function(){});
			}
			else{
				FB.logout(function(){});
				}
			});
			setTimeout(function() {
					window.location.href='http://www.zigwheels.com/logout.php';
			}, 1000); 
			//showWelcome()
	}else{
		deleteFacebookCookies();

		window.location.href='http://www.zigwheels.com/logout.php';
	}
}

	/*del_cookie('fb_user_id', '/', '');
	del_cookie('access_token', '/', '');

	jQuery.post('http://www.zigwheels.com/2db/signOut.php',{},function(data){

			window.location.reload();
		}, 2000);
	});*/
	
}
var popupWindow=null;
function popup(type)
{
	var x = screen.width/2 - 700/2;
    var y = screen.height/2 - 450/2;
	del_cookie("bookmark", '/', '');
	Set_Cookie("bookmark",document.location.href,'','/','','');
	url = 'http://www.zigwheels.com/userreviewlogin.php?tab='+type;
	popupWindow = window.open(url,'parentWindow','width=640,height=480,left='+x+',top='+y);
	if($.browser.safari){ 
		//del_cookie("bookmark", '/', '');
		//Set_Cookie("bookmark",document.location.href,'','/','','');
	}
	else if($.browser.msie){ 
			setInterval(function() {
				if(popupWindow.closed) { 
					var newurl = Get_Cookie("bookmark"); 
					del_cookie("bookmark", '/', '');
					if(newurl!=null && newurl!="undefined" && newurl!=""){
						refreshParent(newurl);
					}else if(checkZWLoginStatus()==1){refreshParent("");}
				}
			}, 10000);
	} else{
		//alert($.browser.mozilla);
	}	
}
function refreshParent(url){
	 	if(url!=null && url!="undefined" && url!=""){
			location.href = url;
		}else { 
			location.reload();
		}
}
function showWelcome(){
	var html;
	
	var userType = Get_Cookie('user_type');
	//alert(userType);
	if(Get_Cookie('user_type')==null){ 
		//var fbSSSOLoginForm='<form name="socialmedia_login" action="http://jsso.indiatimes.com/sso/crossdomain/socialSiteLogin" id="socialmedia_login" method="post"><input type="hidden" name="email" class="email"  value=""><input type="hidden" name="firstname" class="firstname"  value=""><input type="hidden" name="oauthid" class="oauthid"  value=""><input type="hidden" name="oauthsiteid" class="oauthsiteid"  value=""><input type="hidden" name="securitykey" class="securitykey"  value=""><input type="hidden" name="update" value="true"><input name="ru" type="hidden" class="ru"  /><input name="nru" type="hidden" class="nru"  /></form>';
		html ='<div style="float: right; line-height: 25px; padding-top: 0px; font-weight: normal; width: auto;"><a href="javascript:void(0);" class="thickboxnew" id="ssologinlink" onclick="popup(\'individual\')">Sign In</a> | <a href="javascript:void(0);" class="thickboxnew" id="ssoregister" onclick="popup(\'individual\')">Register</a> | <a href="http://www.zigwheels.com/dealer-packages">Dealer Login</a></div>';
	}
	else{
		var userName = Get_Cookie('name');
		userName = userName.replace(/\+/g, ' ');
			
		if(userType=='Dealer') url = "http://www.zigwheels.com/dealer-account";
		else url = "http://www.zigwheels.com/user-account";
		
		//html ='<div style="float: right; line-height: 25px; margin-top:0; font-weight: normal; width: auto;">Welcome '+userName+' | <a href="javascript:void(0)" title="User Logout" onclick="signOut();">Log Out</a> | <a href="'+url+'">My Account</a></span></div>';
		
		html = '<div class="userbox"><ul class="util FL"><li class="tabuser username-cont" onmouseover="showaccnt();" onmouseout="hideaccnt();"><a href="javascript:void(0);" class="tab-name username">'+userName+'<span id="arrow"></span></a><ul class="menuuser"><li class="username"><a href="javascript:void(0)" style="color:#303030">'+userName+'<span id="arrow"></span></a></li><li><a href="'+url+'">My Account</a></li><li><a href="javascript:void(0)" title="User Logout" onclick="signOut();">Logout</a></li></ul></li></ul></div>';

		//signouteverywhere();
	}
	 
	if(document.getElementById('welcomeplaceholder') != null){jQuery('#welcomeplaceholder').html(html);}
	//tb_init('#singin_div_id, #register_div_id');
}

<script>
(function($) {checkSSOLogin()})(jQuery);
function checkSSOLogin(){
var loginstats = checkZWLoginStatus();

var url = 'http://jsso.indiatimes.com/sso/crossdomain/getTicket';
$.ajax({
   type: 'GET',
    url: url,
    async: false,
    contentType: "application/json",
    dataType: 'jsonp',
    success: function(json) { 
	   if(json.ticketId!=""){
		if(loginstats==0){ 
			setCookies(json.ticketId,1);
		}		
	  }else{
			zwsignOut()
	 }
    }
});
}//checkSSOLogin();
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
/*
function removeSocialReader(){
	Set_Cookie( 'social_reader_off', 1, 0, '/');
	Set_Cookie( 'stream_off', 1, 0, '/');
	$('.fbBlock').remove();
}
*/
function toggleSocialReader(val){
	var id = $('#social_selected img').attr('id'); 	//alert(id);
	if(id == "social_on"){
		Set_Cookie('stream_off', 0, 0, '/');
	}else{
		Set_Cookie('stream_off', 1, 0, '/');
	}
}

function getTimeline(val, offset){
	var placeholder_id;
	if(val == 'me'){
		placeholder_id =  'yourfeed';
		var id_next_offset = 'your_feed_next';
		var id_prev_offset = 'your_feed_prev';
		var id_user_name = 'user_name_holder';
	}else{
		placeholder_id =  'friendfeed';
		var id_next_offset = 'friend_next_offset';
		var id_prev_offset = 'friend_prev_offset';
		var id_user_name = 'friend_user_name_holder';
	}
			
		$('#friend_user_name_holder').html('');
		$('#' + placeholder_id).html("<div align=\"center\"><img src=\"http://static.zigwheels.com/images/fb-loader.gif\"/></div>");	
	
		$.post('/submit_to_fb_timeline.php', { 'action' : 'read', 'offset' : offset, 'val' : val }, function(data){
		
		///remove del class for other
		if(val != 'me'){
			$(data).remove('.del');			
		}
				
		$('#' + placeholder_id).html(data);
		var user_name = $('#' + placeholder_id + ' #user_name_fb').val();
		if(val != 'me' && user_name != "" && user_name != undefined){
			$('#' + id_user_name).html(user_name + ',');
		}

		var next_offset = $('#next_offset').val(); //alert(next_offset);
		if(next_offset != ""){
			$('#' + id_next_offset).attr('href', 'javascript:getTimeline("'+ val +'", '+ next_offset +')');
			$('#' + id_next_offset).removeClass('disabled');
		}else{
			$('#' + id_prev_offset).attr('href', 'javascript:void(0)');
			$('#' + id_prev_offset).addClass('disabled');
		}

		var prev_offset = $('#prev_offset').val(); //alert(prev_offset);
		if(prev_offset != ""){
			$('#' + id_prev_offset).attr('href', 'javascript:getTimeline("'+ val +'", '+ prev_offset +')');
			$('#' + id_prev_offset).removeClass('disabled');
		}else{
			$('#' + id_prev_offset ).attr('href', 'javascript:void(0)');
			$('#' + id_prev_offset).addClass('disabled');
		}
	});
}

function deleteFromFbTimeline(id){
	$('#li_' + id).remove();
    
	
	$.post('/submit_to_fb_timeline.php', { 'action' : 'delete', 'id' : id}, function(data){
		$('#li_' + id).remove();
	});
}

function getFriendList(friend_offset){
	
  $.post('/submit_to_fb_timeline.php', {'action':'get_friends', 'friend_offset' : friend_offset}, function(data){
		if(data == ""){
			$('.frnds').attr('style', 'border-bottom:none;');
		}
		$('#friends_response').html(data);
		var next_offset = $('#friendlist_next').val(); //alert(next_offset);
		var prev_offset = $('#friendlist_prev').val();

		if(next_offset != ""){
			$('#friendlist_next_offset').attr('href', 'javascript:getFriendList('+ next_offset +')');
			$('#friendlist_next_offset').removeClass('disabled');
		}else{
			$('#friendlist_next_offset').attr('href', 'javascript:void(0)');
			$('#friendlist_next_offset').addClass('disabled');
		}
	
		if(prev_offset != ""){
			$('#friendlist_prev_offset').attr('href', 'javascript:getFriendList('+ prev_offset +')');
			$('#friendlist_prev_offset').removeClass('disabled');
		}else{
			$('#friendlist_prev_offset').attr('href', 'javascript:void(0)');
			$('#friendlist_prev_offset').addClass('disabled');
		}
	});
}
function getFacebookTemplate(){
		$('#fb_template').html('');
		$('#fb_template').html("<div align=\"center\"><img src=\"http://static.zigwheels.com/images/fb-loader.gif\"/></div>");
			$.ajax({
					type: "GET",
					url: "/tpl/tplRhsFaceBookWidgetTemplate.php",
					cache: false,
					success: function(data){ //alert(data);
			$('#fb_template').html(data);
			getFriendList(0);
			}
		});
		
	}

			message: 'Invite your friends to the new ZigWheels social experience!'
	}, function (response) {
        if (response) {
            console.log(response.toSource());
        } 
    });
}

       	 <script type="text/javascript">
var user_name = 'Full Name';
var user_email = 'Email Address';


var enc_name = Get_Cookie('name');
if(enc_name != null && enc_name != ''){
	user_name = enc_name;	
}

var enc_email = Get_Cookie('email');
if(enc_email != null && enc_email != ''){
jQuery.get('http://www.zigwheels.com/QnAapi/decrypt.php',{"str":enc_email},function(data){
	user_email = data;
	jQuery('#question_user_email').val(user_email);
});
}
function show_galdiv(a)
{

	for(var i=1; i<=3; i++)
	{
		if(i == a){
			document.getElementById('boxgr'+i).className = "act";
			document.getElementById('showdiv'+i).style.display = "block";
		}
		else{
			document.getElementById('boxgr'+i).className = "";
			document.getElementById('showdiv'+i).style.display = "none";
		}
	}
}
function countChar(id,counterid,max,min){
	$("#"+counterid).text("Characters remaining (" + (max - $("#"+id).val().length) + ')');
}

function submitExpertQuestionOnQna(){
var categoryval=jQuery.trim(jQuery('#category').val());
var questiontitleval=jQuery.trim(jQuery('#questiontitle').val());
var question=jQuery.trim(jQuery('#expertquestion').val());
var question_user_name=jQuery.trim(jQuery('#question_user_name').val());
var question_user_email=jQuery.trim(jQuery('#question_user_email').val());
var message;
jQuery('#experterrorpalceholder').hide();
var flag=0;

if(questiontitleval=="" || questiontitleval=='Give title to your question'){
message="Please enter your Question Title.";
jQuery('#experterrorpalceholder').css('display','block');
jQuery('#experterrorpalceholder').html(message);
jQuery('#questiontitle').focus();
flag=1;
}
else if(questiontitleval.length <=19 && questiontitleval!='Give title to your question'){
message="You can not enter less than 20 and more than 160 chars.";
jQuery('#experterrorpalceholder').css('display','block');
jQuery('#experterrorpalceholder').html(message);
jQuery('#questiontitle').focus();
flag=1;
}else if(categoryval==""){
message="Please Choose Category.";
jQuery('#experterrorpalceholder').css('display','block');
jQuery('#experterrorpalceholder').html(message);
//jQuery('#expertquestion').focus();
flag=1;
} else if(question_user_name == "" || question_user_name=='Full Name'){
message="Please enter your Name.";
jQuery('#experterrorpalceholder').css('display','block');
jQuery('#experterrorpalceholder').html(message);
jQuery('#question_user_name').focus();
flag=1;
}else if(question_user_email == "" || question_user_email=='Email Address'){
message="Please enter your Email Address.";
jQuery('#experterrorpalceholder').css('display','block');
jQuery('#experterrorpalceholder').html(message);
jQuery('#question_user_email').focus();
flag=1;
}else if(question_user_email != "" && !isValidEmail(question_user_email)) {
message="Please enter valid Email Address.";
jQuery('#experterrorpalceholder').css('display','block');
jQuery('#experterrorpalceholder').html(message);
jQuery('#question_user_email').focus();
flag=1;
}

if(flag==0){
jQuery.post(TODBFILEPATH+'/putexpertquestion.php', {"question":question,  "category":categoryval, "questiontitle":questiontitleval, "question_user_name":question_user_name, "question_user_email":question_user_email}, function(data){ //alert(data);
jQuery('.error').hide();
document.getElementById('askexpretMsg').style.display = "none";
jQuery('#expertMsg').html(data);
$('#askexpBlock').hide();
jQuery('.conf_msg').show();
});
}	
}
function resetqnaform(){
jQuery('#category').val("");
jQuery('#questiontitle').val("Give title to your question");
jQuery('#expertquestion').val("Describe your question here (optional)");
jQuery('#question_user_name').val(user_name);
jQuery('#question_user_email').val(user_email);

}
function asknewQuestion(){
//jQuery('#experterrorpalceholder').html('');
jQuery('#category').val("");
jQuery('#questiontitle').val("Give title to your question");
jQuery('#expertquestion').val("Describe your question here (optional)");
jQuery('#question_user_name').val(user_name);
jQuery('#question_user_email').val(user_email);
showQuestion();
}
function showQuestion(){
jQuery('#expertMsg').html('');jQuery('.conf_msg').hide();
document.getElementById('askexpretMsg').style.display = "block";
$('#askexpBlock').show();
}

 function setpref()
  {
	
	var value = 0;
	var exdays = 5;
	var exdate=new Date();
	exdate.setDate(exdate.getDate() + exdays);
	var c_value=escape(value) + ((exdays==null) ? "" : ";domain=.zigwheels.com;expires="+exdate.toUTCString());
	document.cookie='vFullSite' + "=" + c_value;
	return true;
		
  }

</script>
